#include "file.h"

void file_readfat(int *fat,unsigned char *img)
{
	int i,j=0;
	for(i=0;i<2880;i+=2)
  2835ee:	83 45 f8 02          	addl   $0x2,-0x8(%ebp)
  2835f2:	81 7d f8 3f 0b 00 00 	cmpl   $0xb3f,-0x8(%ebp)

	}
	return;
